Saw the same Fish Catcher at Carson brand new for $50 but they had a used one they said "Next time you need to catch a fish come borrow our catcher and bring it back."  Carson has been the only shop that doesnt mind testing my water and they do it with a smile.  Instead of saying "oh your good" they tell me exactly what I need to do to get things running 100%.  If you ask for help you get it at Carson.  I also own a retail business and I understand the importance of customer satisfaction.  My hat is off to the guys at Carson Tropical Fish..< /Text><pics>None<//pics><response>None<//response><Gmap_id>0x80dd2dd1fc7cf9f3:0x4d6ea5a17a07bdb<//Gmap_id></record>

<user_id>105350560369406237304<//user_id>< name>
Minh Le</name>
< date>
1341918088472<//date>
<Rating>4< /Rating>< Review>
7.7.2011...I started keeping tropical fish in 1985 and I could immediately tell that this is a bare bones operation for the hardcore hobbyist. If you need frou-frou hand holding and a shiny store just limit your worldview to PetCo and stay there! If you are an experienced reefer with 4+ years experience come here and you will find bargains galore. You need to look past the dust, coralline algae, and salt creep and REALLY LOOK at the corals. It's like going to a club swap, really cool selection with rock bottom prices. The same applies to the used equipment, you have to know what to look for. I bought a used & working 250W HQI MH Nanocube hood for a steal, with ballast included; and tons of SPS & softie frags too for a client's setup. There are good deals on new aquarium packages. The new dry goods selection was okay, but they can always order what you need at fair prices. The marine fish selection was disappointing but I've noticed that many brick & mortar shops have stopped trying to compete against the online retailers on both regards. You're better off going to the shops near LAX for fish. Even Vivid Aquarium, Age of Aquariums, Pacific Reefs and so forth halfheartedly stock fish. Tong's in Fountain Valley has a good fish selection, but only with a 65% survival rate once brought home. I don't even know why Carson Tropical Fish stocks freshwater, they seem like an after thought, but it must be for the neighborhood families and kids. The owner's English isn't the best but there's usually a younger employee around if you have problems communicating. I received excellent service and noticed other customers did as well. I drove over an hour to get to the shop, and albeit off-putting at first, am glad I did. Now it's ranked amongst some of my favorite SoCal LFS's. Give it a try!<//Review>

<Text>Upon initial investigation I discovered this new Chico cookie merchant on the block "crumble" which I assure you their cookies do not do.  At first glance you will notice the abnormally high price of a cookie at this location. After deciding to give a fair review me and my buddy went in on a party pack and made sure to get one of every cookie this week at least for a test, our conclusion is this. At first we didn‚Äôt think much of it, and kept chatting amongst ourselves while we thought about what we wanted to order. We called out ‚Äúhello?‚Äù a few times just to let them know we were ready (bell wasn‚Äôt out, but noticed one further in the kitchen). Still no response. I just did my renewal class today during Covid-19 and I'm super happy with how the class and classroom was set up. There were 5 tables about a little over 6 feet long and spaced more than 6 feet apart.. Each table was set up with 2 stations so a maximum of 10 people this class. I loved that everyone wore masks and were very keen on following social distancing rules. We were provided with gloves to wear during demonstrations and Chlorox wipes to wipe down the props and dummies down after use. Our teacher was very nice and straight forward with the information and demonstrations which was super nice. It made class go by quick. Highly recommend and would totally go back again when it's time for renewal.</Text>

Matthew McGown<//name>
< Text>
Pros-

Autumn is extremely professional.  Even before the class date she reached out via multiple emails highlighting class expectations, materials required and links to materials through the Red Cross.

It did appear that several candidates could not obtain access to the power point presentation in a timely manner but I would say that was on the candidate to communicate that issue to cprtrainingpro.

I thought Autumn. did an incredible job with communication leading up to the class.

I think the class curriculum was great.

She did her best to complete the course within the specified timeline.

That said, the course outline did not allow enough time for breaks.  Adults can only maintain a certain level of attention before needing a break.

Yes , we did break from lecture to activities which does help but I think scheduled defined breaks need to be scheduled and allowed.

Finally, I would strongly recommend that the Company ensure that all (all) manikins and any other tools be in pristine working condition before every class.

If a training tool is non-operational , it needs to be replaced. If the training tool requires batteries, fresh batteries should be installed on a pm schedule to ensure the training tool is 100 percent functional for every class.

As it was pointed out in class to us as potential instructors, people pay a lot of money to take a class and expect all training tools to function.  We as instructor candidates should expect the same.

Autumn needs to identify someone on the team to take on some of these duties like pms for manikins.  I also think this course should have two instructors available during the skills performance section.

Overall, Autumn did an incredible job with our group of 10 individuals with skills ranging from being able to perform instructor duties to individuals that should rethink this path.

I would defiantly recommend Autumn and cprtrainingpro going forward and would use her services for any additional training I may need and/or require.

Best regards,

Matthew McGown< /Text>
